An integrated demo environment allows you to try out the application before connecting to your organisation’s environment.\r\n\r\nWith the CudaLaunch Application you can:\r\n• Connect to a demo environment to try and test the application.\r\n• Use published internal applications (available in the Apps view).\r\n• Add and remove favorites (in the Favorites view) for items you frequently use.\r\n• Automatically launch and connect Remote Desktop sessions.\r\n• Launch SSL Tunnels to use apps on your PC that connect back to your organisation.\r\n• Users can edit their personal information used for accessing internal applications.\r\n• System Administrators are able to enable and disable Dynamic Firewall Rules on the Barracuda CloudGen Firewall.\r\n\r\nCudaLaunch requires Barracuda CloudGen F Firewall version 6.1.1 and higher with the Premium Remote Access subscription.\r\n\r\nTerms: Please see https://www.barracuda.com/legal/software_license_agreement\r\n\r\nAbout Barracuda CloudGen Firewalls\r\nBarracuda CloudGen Firewalls are purpose-built for the modern, distributed network in which network performance and availability is as important as security.
